 aarthik survey yah bhi kahata he ki sarkaar kaa khetiharon kii mushkil dur karne or unki aay ko doguni karne ke lakshya ko puraa karne ke liye lagaataar follow ap karnaa hoga, jisamen kisaanon tak vigyaan or praudyogiki pahunchane ke liye faislakun koshishen bhi kerani hongi

 aarthik surveykshan saaf karata he ki mausam main taapmaana main atyaadhik utaar-chadhaav se kisaanon kii aamadani main kharif kii fasal ke dauraan 4

 1 fisadi rahi he
 While the excess rain brought the income to 13 respectively
 7 or 5
 Reduced by 5 percent
 kisaanon kii aamadani par mausam kii maar acinchit ilaakon main adhik rahi he

 'survey ke mutabik, in saalon main jab taapmaana ausat se ek degree celsius adhik rahaa, varsha sinchit jilon main kharif ke dauraan kisaanon kii aamadani 6

 isi tarah, un varshon main jab barsaat kii maatra ausat se 100 millimetre kam rahi, kisaanon kii aay main kharif ke dauraan 15 fisadi or rabi ke dauraan 7 fisadi kii kami darj kii gai he
 It is estimated that due to climate change, the average income of farmers has decreased by 15 to 18 percent

 vistrut byoraa pesh karte hue dilli ke pashu paalan mantri gopal raay ne kaha ki pichley hafte se rajdhani main mare kul pravasi pakshiyon kii sankhya 18 ho gai he

 philhal nagarikon ko chintaa karne kii jarurat nahin he or keval satarkta baraten

 ' The government fears that the cause of these deaths may be due to H-5 influenza, a cold-related virus that causes bird flu
 raay ne kaha ki chidyaghar se or shahar ke vibhinn pakshi viharon or se murgi bazaaron se 50 namoonay liye hai prayogshaalaon main vishleshan ke liye bheje gaye hai
 Both Delhi's zoos remained closed on Tuesday and Deer Park will remain closed until the situation returns to normal

 Qadir said that at that time Sachin did not say anything and came to bat in front of me in the next over
 mushtak ko pade the 4 chakkeqdir ne bataaya ki sachin ne mere khilaaf agle over main teen chakke maar die

 Words that we can put our words effectively without uttering them

 1
 (completely) surrounded / filled / destroyed / finished / oppositekoi bhi aisi cheez jo bhari ho, ghiri ho, tabah ho yaa puri ho vah puri hi hoti he
 The opposite is not always against, so a modifier is necessary
 2
 (current) trendtrend only means that which is in contemporary and general debate
 3
 (different) kindskinds mean a variety of varieties, which are necessarily different from each other
 4
 Each (and every) Each is specifically meant to be an individual or object
 5
 (empty) The term spacespace refers to an empty space
 jo khaali or kisi ke adhikaar main na ho
 6
 (exact) samesame kaa matlab hi exact hota he
 If something was not exactly the same, we would call it similar

 few (in number) Few speak small number
 alag sandarbh main hamen niyat number kii jarurat padati he

 (first and) foremostforemost kaa matlab hi pehali pojishan hota he

 (foreign) importsimports ke tahat ve saamaan aate hai jo kisivideshi sarajaminse taalluk rakhte hai

 (free) giftparibara par gaur karen to gift kaa matlab hi free hota he

 (genreal) publicpublic kaa matlab hi ordinary people in general arthath aam janata hota he
